  74  * -----------------------------------------------------
  75   
  76  ;
  77   
  78  Parameter
  79   
  80  t(i,j);
  81  *g(i,j) = t(i,j);
  82  Parameter
  83   
  84  c(i,j);
  85  *g(i,j) = c(i,j);
  86   
  87  Equations
  88   
  89  cost        objective function
  90   
  91  constraint1 (i)     xij =1    leave each city only once
  92   
  93  constraint2 (j)     xij =1    arrive at each city only once  ;
  94   
  95  *constraint3 (?)   subtour elimination ;
  96   
  97   
  98  cost..        z=e=sum((i,j),x(i,j)*g(i,j));
  99   
 100   
 101  constraint1(i)..      sum((j)$(not sameas(i,j)),x(i,j)) =e= 1;
 102   
 103  constraint2(j)..      sum((i)$(not sameas(i,j)),x(i,j)) =e= 1;
 104   
 105  Set a(i,j) 'exclude first row and column';
 106  a(i,j) = ord(i) > 1 and ord(j) > 1;
 107   
 108  Variable u(i)     'subtour elimination strategy 3';
 109   
 110  Equation se(i,j) 'subtour elimination constraints';
 111   
 112  se(a(i,j)).. u(i) - u(j) + card(i)*x(i,j) =l= card(i) - 1;
 113   
 114  OPTION OPTCR = 0.05;
 115   
 116  model  Transportation /all/;
 117   
 118  solve Transportation using MIP minimizing z;
 119   
 120  display x.l,z.l;
